<p><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Henry_Rainey" title="Henry Rainey">Henry Rainey</a><br/>
<a href="/wiki/Democratic_Party_(United_States)" title="Democratic Party (United States)">Democratic</a></p>

<p>The <b>1932 United States House of Representatives elections</b> was an election for the <a href="/wiki/United_States_House_of_Representatives" title="United States House of Representatives">United States House of Representatives</a> in 1932 which coincided with the landslide election of <a href="/wiki/President_of_the_United_States" title="President of the United States">President</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Franklin_Delano_Roosevelt" title="Franklin Delano Roosevelt">Franklin Delano Roosevelt</a>.</p>
<p>The inability of <a href="/wiki/Herbert_Hoover" title="Herbert Hoover">Herbert Hoover</a> to cope with the <a href="/wiki/Great_Depression" title="Great Depression">Great Depression</a> was the main issue surrounding this election.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-3"><a href="#cite_note-3">[3]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-4"><a href="#cite_note-4">[4]</a></sup> The overwhelming unpopularity of Hoover caused his <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/United_States_Republican_Party" title="United States Republican Party">Republican Party</a> to lose over 100 seats to Roosevelt's <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/United_States_Democratic_Party" title="United States Democratic Party">Democratic Party</a> and the small <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Minnesota_Farmer-Labor_Party" title="Minnesota Farmer-Labor Party">Farmer-Labor Party</a>. The Democrats retained the majority they had gained through special elections in the last Congress, and expanded it to a commanding level. This round of elections was seen as a referendum on the once popular Republican business practices, which were eschewed for new, more liberal Democratic ideas. This was the first time since <a href="/wiki/United_States_House_of_Representatives_elections,_1894" title="United States House of Representatives elections, 1894">1894</a> that a party suffered triple-digit losses (in this case the Republicans), and the Democrats posted their largest net seat pick-up in history, before or since the election.</p>
<p>Since no reapportionment (and in nearly all states no redistricting) occurred after the 1920 census, the district boundary changes from the previous election are quite substantial, representing twenty years of population movement from small towns to the more Democratic cities.</p>
<p><br/></p>
<p></p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Separate_elections">Separate elections</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=United_States_House_of_Representatives_elections,_1932&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Separate elections">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Two special elections were held apart from those in November. The elected winner would serve only the remainder of the incumbent Congress.</p>

Winner was <a href="#New_Hampshire">subsequently re-elected</a> in November.</td>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="California">California</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=United_States_House_of_Representatives_elections,_1932&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: California">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Nine new seats were added in reapportionment, increasing the delegation from 11 to 20 seats. Six of the new seats were won by Democrats, three by Republicans. Three Republican incumbents lost re-election to Democrats. Therefore, Democrats increased by 10 seats and Republicans decreased by 1.</p>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Indiana"><a href="/wiki/List_of_United_States_Representatives_from_Indiana" title="List of United States Representatives from Indiana">Indiana</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=United_States_House_of_Representatives_elections,_1932&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Indiana">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Indiana gained one seat in reapportionment. All of the incumbents were redistricted. The new seat was won by a Democrat and all the other incumbent Democrats won re-election. All three incumbent Republicans lost re-election, bringing the state from 8-3 Democratic to 12-0 Democratic.</p>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Kansas"><a href="/wiki/List_of_United_States_Representatives_from_Kansas" title="List of United States Representatives from Kansas">Kansas</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=United_States_House_of_Representatives_elections,_1932&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: Kansas">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The eighth district was eliminated when the state was reapportioned from eight to seven districts. Two incumbent Republicans lost re-election. One incumbent Republican lost renomination and his seat was won by the incumbent Democrat from the district that was merged into his.</p>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Kentucky"><a href="/wiki/List_of_United_States_Representatives_from_Kentucky" title="List of United States Representatives from Kentucky">Kentucky</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=United_States_House_of_Representatives_elections,_1932&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: Kentucky">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Kentucky, reapportioned from 11 districts down to 9, elected all of its representatives on a statewide at-large ticket. Of the nine incumbent Democratic representatives, seven were re-elected on the general ticket and two retired, while both incumbent Republicans retired.</p>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Louisiana"><a href="/wiki/List_of_United_States_Representatives_from_Louisiana" title="List of United States Representatives from Louisiana">Louisiana</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=United_States_House_of_Representatives_elections,_1932&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: Louisiana">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Louisiana continued to elect its representatives based upon districts adopted in 1912. Those districts did not change until the 1968 elections.</p>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Maine"><a href="/wiki/List_of_United_States_Representatives_from_Maine" title="List of United States Representatives from Maine">Maine</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=United_States_House_of_Representatives_elections,_1932&amp;action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit section: Maine">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Maine was redistricted from four seats down to three; of four Republican incumbents, only one was re-elected; one retired and two were defeated by Democratic challengers.</p>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Massachusetts"><a href="/wiki/List_of_United_States_Representatives_from_Massachusetts" title="List of United States Representatives from Massachusetts">Massachusetts</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=United_States_House_of_Representatives_elections,_1932&amp;action=edit&amp;section=22" title="Edit section: Massachusetts">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Massachusetts was redistricted from 16 districts to 15; 10 Republican and 4 Democratic incumbents were re-elected, while 2 Republican incumbents retired in the old 8th and 9th districts; the new 8th containing parts of both elected a Democrat.</p>
<table class="wikitable">
<tr valign="bottom">
<th>District</th>
<th>Incumbent</th>
<th>Party</th>
<th>First<br/>
elected</th>
<th>Result</th>
<th>Candidates</th>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><a href="/wiki/Massachusetts%27s_1st_congressional_district" title="Massachusetts's 1st congressional district">Massachusetts 1</a></td>
<td><a href="/wiki/Allen_T._Treadway" title="Allen T. Treadway">Allen T. Treadway</a></td>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Michigan"><a href="/wiki/List_of_United_States_Representatives_from_Michigan" title="List of United States Representatives from Michigan">Michigan</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=United_States_House_of_Representatives_elections,_1932&amp;action=edit&amp;section=23" title="Edit section: Michigan">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Michigan was redistricted from 13 to 17 districts, adding four new districts in and around Detroit.</p>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Minnesota"><a href="/wiki/List_of_United_States_Representatives_from_Minnesota" title="List of United States Representatives from Minnesota">Minnesota</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=United_States_House_of_Representatives_elections,_1932&amp;action=edit&amp;section=24" title="Edit section: Minnesota">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Minnesota, reapportioned from 10 seats down to 9, elected all representatives on a statewide general ticket. Of 10 incumbents, 1 Farmer-Labor and 1 Republican were re-elected, 4 Republicans lost re-election, 3 Republicans lost renomination, and 1 Republican retired.</p>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Missouri"><a href="/wiki/List_of_United_States_Representatives_from_Missouri" title="List of United States Representatives from Missouri">Missouri</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=United_States_House_of_Representatives_elections,_1932&amp;action=edit&amp;section=26" title="Edit section: Missouri">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Missouri was reapportioned from 16 seats to 13, which were elected on a general ticket. The delegation went from 12 Democrats and 4 Republicans to 13 Democrats, 8 of them previous incumbents.</p>
